  445. I read reviews about some pieces being missing in some people's kits but decided to risk it simply based on the fact that all comments mentioned that they had been able to easily request a replacement or missing pieces. I will put the short version or &#34;tl;dr&#34; (too long; didn't read) first but I recommend anyone interested in buying this product read the full thing. TL;DR Version: This is a purchase I am happy I made, I would recommend it to my friends but I wish they gave some instruction on what each tool is for and how to clean them with the kit. It should be used as a secondary tool when compared to normal cleaners and should be used with warm/hot and cold water for best effectiveness. Favorite application for it has to be the easy and relieving removal of painful blemishes that can appear suddenly. FULL VERSION: Fair warning, I am reviewing this in a manner that will mention (in general, not graphically or detailed) &#34;popped&#34; or removed/reduced zits and other issues. If picturing these can bother you this review (and likely this kit) is not for you and I recommend sticking with the shortened version above. Pros: 1) This kit works b-e-a-utifully for the pimples or zits that can sometimes appear near points of lots of movement (lips, right below nose, etc) that are normally very painful if left alone. This kit allows the swelling to be safely and easily removed / reduced without pinching which would normally irritate the skin and still hurt for a while after. 2) For blackheads or clogged pores (the nose, specifically), I have found that this is a great secondary tool. Rather than relying on this kit as a primary removal tool, for the nose I would recommend the stick-on Biore nose strips (or a similar brand / tool) being used first. 2-A) After the &#34;blanket&#34; tool of the strip / cleanser has been used, I use this kit to get any of the remaining or partially-removed obstructions in my pores. I HIGHLY recommend cleaning any of the strips left-behind adhesive residue with warm/hot water before using this kit. This is to prevent any left-over strip stuff from reclogging your pores (Duh[?]) and to open your pores again because they likely closed while waiting for the strips to dry. 3) BUT WAIT! THERE'S MORE! Something that I had not considered when I purchased the kit was just how useful it would be for those dreaded ingrown hairs from shaving or occasionally on the legs. The tool in the middle (in the current thumbnail / image) has an end that is shaped like a small soup spoon with a hole in the middle that, in combination with tweezers (usually, but not always needed), made getting ingrown hairs removed super simple with any mirror available to you. This is saved me a lot of time and prevented a lot of (figurative) hair-pulling by making (literal) hair-pulling very simple by isolating the (evil and hateful) hair or damaged follicle and presenting it as an easy target for tweezers (or fingers if you are feeling like Tom Hank's Castaway). 4) The kit does everything that it advertises and keeps your skin from swelling or having discoloration due to pinching, but also allows me to not have to &#34;wait out&#34; a pimple before going out in public. 5) The built-in cloth that is in the case makes it very easy and handy to dry tools after sterilization. It is not easily seen in the thumbnail picture, but it is the black part extending to the right and it fits very easily back into the case. I do not know if that is its intended function, but it has worked great for me in this way. 6) Despite all user-based instructions and time-learned techniques suggesting to clear the blemish / wound until there is some visible blood to completely clear it; I have also found that after using this kit instead of my fingers has led to a massive decrease in the chance of scabbing. Normally, the eliminated target would have a fairly high risk of scabbing because of &#34;heavy&#34; bleeding relative to the wound. This scabbing would often lead to picking for many people, even unintentionally, only making the issue worse. Many times, the spot that is healing could potentially look worse than if left alone. 7) As yet another (somewhat gross) bonus it allows me to indulge in the guilty pleasure of popping and removing the zits on my face that would normally have to be done with my fingers (if it were required, like in cases of being painful or uncomfortable) and would only serve to further aggravate my skin / pores. Admit it, we all go back to our pre-teen roots sometimes with these blemishes on our face and have a feeling of satisfaction in eliminating them. Cons and suggestions to seller: 1) Methods for proper sterilization (which is VERY important) are not given and must be found online or elsewhere. A printed paper that showed easy or recommended ways to sterilize the tools would be appreciated. A quick Google search did the job, but it would have been awesome to not need to search it at all. I can understand though where they might not do this in order to avoid issues with sterilization &#34;not working&#34; or some other liability issue though. 2) Each tools proper or intended use is not given, which can add a small learning curve as to what works best and where. **Only (potentially) applies to those who may travel a lot with the kit.** 3) I am not sure if much can really be done (realistically) on the seller's part, but the longest tool in the set has a poky end that sometimes likes to try and stick through the casing and could potentially cause issues by stabbing through something else in a travel bag or something. However, this has not occurred to me more than once or twice and the first time I noticed it was when I originally opened it after it was shipped to me. Just a fair word of warning though. I have found that a nicer quality zip-loc sandwich bag is enough of a buffer to prevent and issues with this problem. **SUMMARY** Overall, this is a great kit that I have been using every chance it is required. It is a superior alternative to the pinch and pray technique that many of us are used to, provided you (even occasionally, provided it is lightly used) clean, sterilize, and maintain the tools. It easily eliminates zits/pimples, helps remove or fix ingrown hairs, and clears obstructions in the pores of your nose. For the nose, a bit more force is usually needed than elsewhere on the face if you want to really get everything out, which may still cause some redness / swelling or pain shortly after. Despite all of the positive feelings and utility of this kit, I do not feel that it should be used as a primary tool when taking care of or cleaning your face. Strips / cleansers should be used first, along with the application or pore-opening warm / hot water. This kit should be used after applying warm-water to open the pores. Then, after using the kit, it is recommended that you then use pore-closing agents / cleaners to reduce the chances of the now clear pores being clogged again. The cheapest and most recommended pore-closer being cold water. However, I wish they gave some basic instructions with the kit: including proper cleaning/sterilization and each tools suited purpose, but all pieces were in the kit and work great together. These issues can be fixed with both a Google search or Youtube search, but I would like to not need these as a matter of convenience. The lack of providing this information, while somewhat minor, is what made me knock off a star (can't do 4 1/2). This kit has allowed me to properly manage the blemishes on my face without having to deal with the usual issues that came with pinching, including redness, bleeding and scabbing, swelling or irritation of skin after pinching, and has ultimately been a very satisfying purchase that I wish I had made earlier in life. However, I have it now and I am glad it caught my eye while browsing.isfying purchase that I wish I had made earlier in life. However, I have it now and I am glad it caught my eye while browsing.
